NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
 
K. Arunmalraj, a male child born to Thiru M.R.Karuppasamy, on 27th June 1994, residing at 7/125, 11th Street,
Shanthinagar, Palayamkottai, Tirunelveli District-627 005, has been living as a Female. She has been granted an Identity
card No. TVL/001/2018 issued by the Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department
By this I, may be treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as K. APSARA
Tirunelveli, 
K. ARUNMALRAJ 
 
2nd March 2020. 
 
Balasubramaniyam, a male child born to Thiru Kuppannakunder, on 10th July 1956, residing at 13-C, Bharathi Nagar 
3rd Street, Uppilipalayam, Coimbatore South, Coimbatore-641 015, has been living as a Female. She has been granted an 
Identity card No.CBE/046/2018 issued by the Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social welfare and NMP Department.
By this I, may be treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as NANDHINI
Coimbatore, 
BALASUBRAMANIYAM  
2nd March 2020.
 
G. Anbu Rajan, a male child born to Thiru A. Gandhi on 25th May 1985 residing at No.64, HMS colony, Ramalingam
Nagar, Arasureddy, Theni Main Road, Madurai-625 016. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery she has been living as a 
female (reference Dr. V. Jayaraman, MS,Mch,MNAMS,Dip,NB,Phd,FlCS, professor head dept of burns, plastic and reconstructive 
surgery, Government Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010.) By this I, could be treated as a female, and shall henceforth 
be known as G.OORVASI.
Madurai,  
G. ANBU RAJAN 
 
4th March 2020.
 
K. Saravanan, a male child born to Thiru. E. Kamalakannan 9th November 1986, residing at No.6, 2nd Cross Street, 
Kamachi Nagar, Maduravoyal, Chennai-600 095. has been living has a female. She has been granted an Identify card
No. CHN/087/2018 Issued by the Tamil Nadu Transgender Welfare Board, Social welfare and NMP Department. By this I, may be 
treated as female and shall henceforth be known as K. SAROJA.
Chennai, 
K. SARAVANAN  
5th March 2020.
 
 
O. Sivagurunathan, a male child born to Thiru Oyyaram.M, on 18th May 1990, residing at 46/18, Aniyappur, Aniyappur 
Post, Manapparai Taluk, Tiruchirappalli District-621 307, has been living as a Female. She has been granted an Identity card 
No.KPM/092/2019 issued by the Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. By this I, may be 
treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as O. SHIVARANJANI
